 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;2.02. Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On February&#160;28, 2022, iCAD, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release announcing its financial results for the quarter and year ended December&#160;31, 2021. A copy of the Company&#8217;s press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Exhibit 99.1 is being furnished pursuant to Item 2.02, is not to be considered filed under the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), and shall not be incorporated by reference into any of the Company&#8217;s previous or future filings under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;9.01 Financial Statements and Exhibits. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) Exhibits </p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>iCAD REPORTS FINANCIAL RESULTS FOR FOURTH QUARTER AND YEAR ENDED DECEMBER&nbsp;31, 2021 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Launched ProFound AI<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> Risk, the world&#146;s first clinical decision support tool
for short term breast cancer risk estimation </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Demonstrated compelling survival data for the use of Xoft<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> Brain IORT in recurrent glioblastoma (GBM) as published in Surgical Neurology International </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>-&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Company to Host Conference Call&nbsp;&amp; Webcast Today at 4:30 PM ET&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>NASHUA, N.H. &#150; February</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;28, 2022 &#150;</B> iCAD, Inc. (NASDAQ: ICAD),&nbsp;a global medical technology leader providing innovative
cancer detection and therapy solutions, today reported its financial and operating results for the three and 12 months ended December&nbsp;31, 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Revenues for the three-month and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">12-month</FONT> periods ended December&nbsp;31, 2021 were $7.8&nbsp;million and
$33.6&nbsp;million, respectively, compared to $10.5&nbsp;million and $29.7&nbsp;million in the three- and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">12-month</FONT> periods ended December&nbsp;31, 2020, respectively. Net loss for the three-month and <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">12-month</FONT> periods ended December&nbsp;31, 2021, were $4.1&nbsp;million and $11.2&nbsp;million, respectively, compared to $1.6&nbsp;million and $17.6&nbsp;million in the three- and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">12-month</FONT> periods ended December&nbsp;31, 2020, respectively. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Recent Highlights: </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Accelerated the adaptation of commercial operations to evolving market trends in order to maximize access to
iCAD&#146;s large addressable markets </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Appointed Dana Brown and Timothy Norris, who each offer significant insight and decades of relevant experience in
corporate leadership, brand stewardship, and health technologies, as well as proven track records of leading innovation and strategic change, to the Board of Directors </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Signed a global distribution agreement with Arterys, the world&#146;s leading vendor-neutral AI platform, to
launch Arterys&#146; AI SaaS solution </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Granted an Authorization to Operate from the U.S. Department of Defense for its breast AI platform
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;As it affected many segments of the global economy, the surge in the Omicron variant in December had a negative impact on our
customers in the fourth quarter,&#148; said Stacey Stevens, incoming CEO. &#147;Customer focus on surging <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> infection rates, severe staffing shortages and resource limitations made the processing of new
purchase orders challenging, resulting in the postponement of several, larger enterprise deals in the quarter. The effects of this recent variant were also felt within our own team, as approximately 1/3 of our global sales staff was afflicted with <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> in December.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Two months into 2022, we are encouraged to see some gradual improvements in the
market,&#148; continued Stevens. &#147;As the Omicron surge is subsiding, we are seeing customers beginning to focus more on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-COVID</FONT> related business decisions.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We are currently at an important and exciting inflection point in the Company from both a product and operational perspective,&#148; said Stevens.
&#147;We have a robust portfolio of superior technologies for the detection, risk assessment, and treatment of breast and other cancers and we are operating in large, under-penetrated markets with superior clinical and economic value propositions
that are making a major contribution towards better patient care.&#148; </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;A key theme for us this year is the focus on driving increased revenue and growth from our existing
portfolio of leading solutions. To this end, we are enhancing our commercial sales infrastructure, sharpening our focus to maximize our access to the entirety of our large addressable market, and helping customers to adopt our technologies more
flexibly,&#148; concluded Stevens. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Fourth Quarter 2021 Financial Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Total Detection and Therapy revenue for the fourth quarter of 2021 was $7.8&nbsp;million, a decrease of $2.6&nbsp;million, or 25%, as compared to the fourth
quarter of 2020, reflecting a 38% decline in product revenue, offset by 10% growth in service and supplies revenue. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

density products, and the associated service and supplies revenue, decreased by approximately $2.6&nbsp;million, or 32%, as compared to the fourth quarter of 2020. Therapy revenue for the fourth quarter of 2021, which includes Xoft<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> Axxent<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> eBx<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> System<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP>
sales, as well as the associated service and supplies revenue, decreased by $0.04&nbsp;million, or 1%, as compared to the fourth quarter of 2020. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

9.9&nbsp;million, a $0.9&nbsp;million, or 10%, increase from $ 9.0&nbsp;million in the fourth quarter of 2020. </P>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">GAAP Net Loss: Net loss for the fourth quarter of 2021 was ($4.1) million, or ($0.17) per diluted share, as
compared to a net loss of ($1.6) million, or ($0.07) per diluted share, for the fourth quarter of 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT>
Adjusted Net Loss: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> adjusted net loss, a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure as defined below, for the fourth quarter of 2021 was ($4.1) million, or ($0.17) per diluted
share, as compared to a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjusted net loss of ($1.4) million, or ($0.06) per diluted share, for the fourth quarter of 2020. Please refer to the section entitled &#147;Reconciliation of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP Measures&#148; and the accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a reconciliation of GAAP Net Loss to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss results for the three-month periods ended December&nbsp;31, 2021 and 2020, respectively. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> adjusted EBITDA, a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure as defined below, for the fourth quarter of 2021 was a loss of ($3.3) million, a $2.4&nbsp;million increase as compared to the fourth quarter 2020
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjusted EBITDA loss of ($0.9) million. Please refer to the section entitled &#147;Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP
Measures&#148; and the accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a reconciliation of GAAP Net Loss to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA results for the three-month periods ended
December&nbsp;31, 2021 and 2020, respectively. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Twelve months ended December&nbsp;31, 2021 Financial Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Total Detection and Therapy revenue for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2021, was $33.6&nbsp;million, an increase of $3.9&nbsp;million, or 13.3%, as compared
to the same period of 2020, reflecting a 12.1% increase in product revenue, and a 15.3% increase in service and supplies revenue. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

density products, and the associated service and supplies revenue, remained relatively consistent at $22&nbsp;million, as compared to the same period of 2020. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Therapy revenue for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2021, which includes Xoft<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> Axxent<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> eBx<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> System<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> sales, as well as the associated service and supplies revenue,
increased by $3.9&nbsp;million, or 50.9%, as compared to the same period of 2020. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross Profit: Gross profit for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2021 was $24.2&nbsp;million, or 72.1% of
revenue, as compared to $21.4&nbsp;million, or 71.9% of revenue, in the same period of 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating Expenses: Total operating expenses for the year
ended December&nbsp;31, 2021 were $35.0&nbsp;million, an increase of $4.3&nbsp;million or 13.8%, compared to $30.7&nbsp;million in the same period of 2020. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">GAAP Net Loss: Net loss for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2021, was ($11.2) million, or ($0.45) per diluted share, as compared to a net loss of ($17.6)
million, or ($0.80) per diluted share, for the same period of 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss: <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> adjusted net loss, a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure as defined below, for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2021, was ($10.7) million, or ($0.43) per diluted share, as
compared to a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> adjusted net loss of ($9.5) million, or ($0.43) per diluted share, for the same period of 2020. Please refer to the section entitled &#147;Reconciliation of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP Measures&#148; and the accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a reconciliation of GAAP Net Loss to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss results for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2021 and 2020, respectively. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> adjusted EBITDA, a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure as defined below, for the year ended December&nbsp;31,
2021, was a loss of ($7.3) million, a $1.5&nbsp;million increase compared to the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2020, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjusted EBITDA loss of ($5.7) million. Please refer to the section entitled
&#147;Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP Measures&#148; and the accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a reconciliation of GAAP Net Loss to <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA results for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2021 and 2020, respectively. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cash and Cash
Equivalents: As of December&nbsp;31, 2021, the Company had cash and cash equivalents of $34.3&nbsp;million, compared to cash and cash equivalents of $27.2&nbsp;million at December&nbsp;31, 2020. </P>
